# e/g max Iso vs |ieta| and nTT
# Index is compressedIeta<<8+compressedE<<4+compressednTT.
# Cuts corresponding to 50%+50%*ET/70 GeV efficiency.
# PU dependence is treated with fixed iso. cut dependence on nTT : iso. cut(nTT) = iso. cut(nTT=16) + (nTT-16)/5
#anything after # is ignored with the exception of the header
#the header is first valid line starting with #<header> versionStr(unused but may be in future) nrBitsAddress nrBitsData </header>
#<header> V3 12 9 </header>
